                        <div class="WhatToDo">
                        <h1 class="Header-title">Bad Gateway</h1>
                        <p>If that is not the case, take a look at the article on <a href="https://client.cdn77.com/support/knowledgebase/cdn-resource/troubleshooting-error-messages" class="common-link">troubleshooting error messages</a> in our knowledgebase.</p>
                        <p>Please make sure the firewall on your origin server is disabled. It might be blocking the requests from the CDN77 servers.</p>
                        <p>Please try again in a few minutes. If the problem persists for more than 30 minutes, try contacting website owner via a different channel.</p>
